Since the Validate process may access the shared Paymaster, 

there are some nepotistic effects, such as some Dos attacks ^uKn81pyN

We use a reputation system to enable Bundler to check the frequency of 

authentication failures by Paymaster and to prevent Sybil attacks by Paymaster, 

Paymaster is also required to perform Stake on Entry Point. ^KQPWnwgH
